-- insert into table

declare @StartValue int;
set @StartValue=(select last_num from new_num where table_name = 'pr_ob_share');

insert into pr_ob_share(id,[emp_id]
           ,[emp_code]
           ,[fy]
           ,[fm]
           ,[active]
           ,[trans_id]
           ,[own_share_total]
           ,[vpf_total]
           ,[bank_share_total]) 
select @StartValue+ROW_NUMBER() OVER(ORDER BY emp_code) AS Row,[emp_id]
           ,[emp_code]
           ,[fy]
           ,[fm]
           ,[active]
           ,[trans_id]
           ,[own_share_total]
           ,[vpf_total]
           ,[bank_share_total] from pr_ob_share_temp

declare @lastnum int;
set @lastnum = (select top 1 id from pr_ob_share order by id desc)
update new_num set last_num=@lastnum where table_name='pr_ob_share'




--drop 
drop table pr_ob_share_temp;
